% maxwidth is the original width if it is less than linewidth
% otherwise use linewidth (to make sure the graphics do not exceed the margin)
\makeatletter
\def\maxwidth{ %
  \ifdim\Gin@nat@width>\linewidth
    \linewidth
  \else
    \Gin@nat@width
  \fi
}
\makeatother

\definecolor{fgcolor}{rgb}{0.345, 0.345, 0.345}
\newcommand{\hlnum}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.686,0.059,0.569}{#1}}%
\newcommand{\hlstr}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.192,0.494,0.8}{#1}}%
\newcommand{\hlcom}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.678,0.584,0.686}{\textit{#1}}}%
\newcommand{\hlopt}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0,0,0}{#1}}%
\newcommand{\hlstd}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.345,0.345,0.345}{#1}}%
\newcommand{\hlkwa}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.161,0.373,0.58}{\textbf{#1}}}%
\newcommand{\hlkwb}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.69,0.353,0.396}{#1}}%
\newcommand{\hlkwc}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.333,0.667,0.333}{#1}}%
\newcommand{\hlkwd}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.737,0.353,0.396}{\textbf{#1}}}%
\let\hlipl\hlkwb

\usepackage{framed}
\makeatletter
\newenvironment{kframe}{%
 \def\at@end@of@kframe{}%
 \ifinner\ifhmode%
  \def\at@end@of@kframe{\end{minipage}}%
  \begin{minipage}{\columnwidth}%
 \fi\fi%
 \def\FrameCommand##1{\hskip\@totalleftmargin \hskip-\fboxsep
 \colorbox{shadecolor}{##1}\hskip-\fboxsep
     % There is no \\@totalrightmargin, so:
     \hskip-\linewidth \hskip-\@totalleftmargin \hskip\columnwidth}%
 \MakeFramed {\advance\hsize-\width
   \@totalleftmargin\z@ \linewidth\hsize
   \@setminipage}}%
 {\par\unskip\endMakeFramed%
 \at@end@of@kframe}
\makeatother

\definecolor{shadecolor}{rgb}{.97, .97, .97}
\definecolor{messagecolor}{rgb}{0, 0, 0}
\definecolor{warningcolor}{rgb}{1, 0, 1}
\definecolor{errorcolor}{rgb}{1, 0, 0}
\newenvironment{knitrout}{}{} % an empty environment to be redefined in TeX

\usepackage{alltt}

\usepackage{xcolor}
\usepackage{graphicx, tikz}



\newlength{\cardwidthspace}
\newlength{\cardheightspace}
\newlength{\cardmargin}
\setlength{\cardmargin}{0pt}% default => two side printing <<<<<<<<<<<<<<<

\setlength{\cardwidthspace}{18pt} % add right horizontal space
\setlength{\cardheightspace}{20pt}% add upper vertical space

% \setlength{\cardmargin}{\cardwidthspace}  % use for one side printing <<<<<<<<<<<<<<<           

\usepackage{etoolbox}   % for the patch 
\patchcmd{\card}
{\front\noindent\begin{picture}(0,0)}
{\front\noindent\begin{picture}(0,0)\advance\cardwidth by -\cardwidthspace\relax\advance\cardheight by -\cardheightspace\relax}
{}{}

\patchcmd{\card}
{\back\noindent\begin{picture}(0,0)}
{\back\noindent\begin{picture}(0,0)%
        \advance\cardwidth by -\cardwidthspace\relax%
        \advance\cardheight by -\cardheightspace\relax%
        \advance\@tempdimb by \cardmargin\relax% 
    }
{}{}

\renewcommand{\cardtextstylef}{\ttfamily \bfseries \large}
\renewcommand{\cardtextstyleb}{\ttfamily \bfseries \large}

\newcommand{\flashcard}[1]{% create new command for cards with blanks
    \card{% call the original \card command with twice the same argument (#1)
        \let\blank\frontcard% but let \blank behave like \frontcard the first time
        #1
    }{%
        \let\blank\backcard% and like \backcard the second time
        #1
    }%
}

%% Set front head & back foot for dfs
\renewcommand{\flhead}{\vskip5pt \fboxsep=0pt {\small\bfseries\footnotesize Nafnorð | 名词}}
\renewcommand{\fcfoot}{\vskip5pt \fboxsep=0pt \hspace{2pt}{\small\bfseries\footnotesize 3K}}

\renewcommand{\blhead}{\vskip5pt {\small\bfseries\footnotesize Nafnorð | 名词 }}
\renewcommand{\bcfoot}{\vskip5pt \hspace{2pt}{\small\bfseries\footnotesize 3K}}


%% card templates
\card{\Large{umboðsmaður} \normalsize{\textsubscript{(\textit{m.})}} \\ [2ex]
{Þá hefur \textcolor{red}{\underline{umboðsmaður}} Alþingis óskað eftir upplýsingum um málið. }}
{umboðsmaður \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{m.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side
\textphonetic{[ʏmpɔðsmaðʏr]} \\
zh: \emph{代理人} \\  [2ex]
\renewcommand*{\arraystretch}{0.8}
\makebox[0.9\cardwidth]{
\begin{tabular}{l l}
\textsc{sg}: & (frá) umboðsmanni -- (til) umboðsmanns \\ 
\textsc{pl}: & (frá) umboðsmönnum -- (til) umboðsmanna \\
\end{tabular}}
}

{Utanríkisráðuneytið hefur nú kynnt í \textcolor{red}{\underline{grófum}} dráttum niðurskurðartillögur sínar. }}
{grófur \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{adj.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side
\textphonetic{[krouːvʏr]} \\
zh: \emph{粗糙的} \\  [2ex]
\renewcommand*{\arraystretch}{0.8}
\makebox[0.9\cardwidth]{
\begin{tabular}{ll}
\textsc{pos}: & grófur  --  gróf -- gróft \\ 
\textsc{comp}: & grófari -- grófari -- grófara \\ 
\textsc{superl}: & grófastur -- grófust -- grófast \\
\end{tabular}}
}

{losun \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{f.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side

\end{tabular}}

%% card templates

{Hann sagði að staðan sem væri komin upp væri engin \textcolor{red}{\underline{tilviljun}} . }}
{tilviljun \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{f.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side

\end{tabular}}

{grunur \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{m.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side

\begin{tabular}{l l}

\textsc{pl}: & (frá)  -- (til)  \\
\end{tabular}}
}

{áttundi \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{num.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side

zh: \emph{第八} \\  [2ex]

\end{tabular}

{elta \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{v.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side

\textsc{3sg}: & eltir -- elti -- elt \\ 
\end{tabular}
}

\end{tabular}}

{Fyrsta skrefið sé þó að taka upp \textcolor{red}{\underline{þráðinn}} með íþróttafélaginu. }}
{þráður \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{m.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side
\textphonetic{[θrauːðʏr]} \\
zh: \emph{线} \\  [2ex]
\renewcommand*{\arraystretch}{0.8}
\makebox[0.9\cardwidth]{
\begin{tabular}{l l}
\textsc{sg}: & (frá) þræði -- (til) þráðar \\ 
\textsc{pl}: & (frá) þráðum -- (til) þráða \\
\end{tabular}}
}

%% card templates
\card{\Large{flugfélag} \normalsize{\textsubscript{(\textit{n.})}} \\ [2ex]
{Vetrarhörkur hafa sett strik í reikninginn hjá mörgum \textcolor{red}{\underline{flugfélögum}} í Evrópu. }}
{flugfélag \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{n.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side
\textphonetic{[flʏxfjɛlaɣ]} \\
zh: \emph{航空公司} \\  [2ex]
\renewcommand*{\arraystretch}{0.8}
\makebox[0.9\cardwidth]{
\begin{tabular}{l l}
\textsc{sg}: & (frá) flugfélagi -- (til) flugfélags \\ 
\textsc{pl}: & (frá) flugfélögum -- (til) flugfélaga \\
\end{tabular}}
}

%% card templates
\card{\Large{málflutningur} \normalsize{\textsubscript{(\textit{m.})}} \\ [2ex]
{Engin opinber gögn styðji \textcolor{red}{\underline{málflutning}} ráðamanna. }}
{málflutningur \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{m.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side
\textphonetic{[maulflʏhtniŋkʏr]} \\
zh: \emph{陈述，陈述一个案例} \\  [2ex]

\begin{tabular}{l l}
\textsc{sg}: & (frá) málflutningi -- (til) málflutnings \\ 
\textsc{pl}: & (frá)  -- (til)  \\
\end{tabular}}
}
